    /**
     * Generate code for the given tree. The trees should contain statements
     * and not produce any value. Use genLoad for expressions which leave
     * a value on top of the stack.
     *
     * @param tree ...
     * @param ctx  ...
     * @return a new context. This is necessary for control flow instructions
     *         which may change the current basic block.
     */

        ICodePhase.this.Contextcase Assign(GenICode.this.global.Selectlhs @ Select(_, _), GenICode.this.global.Treerhs) =>

            ICodePhase.this.Contextctx1
          } else {
            var ICodePhase.this.Contextctx1 = (GenICode.this.global.Tree,ICodePhase.this.Context)ICodePhase.this.ContextgenLoadQualifier(GenICode.this.global.Selectlhs, ICodePhase.this.Contextctx)
            ICodePhase.this.Contextctx1 = (GenICode.this.global.Tree,ICodePhase.this.Context,GenICode.this.global.icodes.TypeKind)ICodePhase.this.ContextgenLoad(GenICode.this.global.Treerhs, ICodePhase.this.Contextctx1, (GenICode.this.global.icodes.global.Type)GenICode.this.global.icodes.TypeKindtoTypeKind(GenICode.this.global.Selectlhs.=> GenICode.this.global.Symbolsymbol.=> GenICode.this.global.Typeinfo))

          val ICodePhase.this.Contextctx1 = (GenICode.this.global.Tree,ICodePhase.this.Context,GenICode.this.global.icodes.TypeKind)ICodePhase.this.ContextgenLoad(GenICode.this.global.Treerhs, ICodePhase.this.Contextctx, (GenICode.this.global.icodes.global.Type)GenICode.this.global.icodes.TypeKindtoTypeKind(GenICode.this.global.Treelhs.=> GenICode.this.global.Symbolsymbol.=> GenICode.this.global.Typeinfo))

    /**
     * Generate code for trees that produce values on the stack
     *
     * @param tree The tree to be translated
     * @param ctx  The current context
     * @param expectedType The type of the value to be generated on top of the
     *                     stack.
     * @return The new context. The only thing that may change is the current 
     *         basic block (as the labels map is mutable).
     */

        (AnyRef)Unitlog(java.lang.String("at line: ")"at line: " (Any)java.lang.String+ (GenICode.this.global.Treetree.=> scala.tools.nsc.util.Positionpos).=> Option[Int]line.((Int) => java.lang.String)Option[java.lang.String]map(Int_.()java.lang.StringtoString).(=> java.lang.String)java.lang.StringgetOrElse(GenICode.this.global.Treetree.=> scala.tools.nsc.util.Positionpos.()java.lang.StringtoString))

      /**
       * Generate code for primitive arithmetic operations.
       */

        val (GenICode.this.global.Select, GenICode.this.global.Tree, List[GenICode.this.global.Tree])Apply(GenICode.this.global.Selectfun @ Select(GenICode.this.global.Treelarg, _), List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]args) = GenICode.this.global.Treetree

        var GenICode.this.global.icodes.TypeKindresKind = (GenICode.this.global.icodes.global.Type)GenICode.this.global.icodes.TypeKindtoTypeKind(GenICode.this.global.Treelarg.=> GenICode.this.global.Typetpe)

        Unitif (=> scala.tools.nsc.Settingssettings.=> scala.tools.nsc.Settings.BooleanSettingdebug.=> scala.tools.nsc.Settings.BooleanSetting#Tvalue) {

        }

        List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]args Unitmatch {
          // unary operation
          Unitcase object NilNil =>
            ICodePhase.this.Contextctx1 = (GenICode.this.global.Tree,ICodePhase.this.Context,GenICode.this.global.icodes.TypeKind)ICodePhase.this.ContextgenLoad(GenICode.this.global.Treelarg, ICodePhase.this.Contextctx1, GenICode.this.global.icodes.TypeKindresKind)
            Intcode Unitmatch {
              Unitcase scalaPrimitives.Int(1)POS =>

    /**
     * Returns a list of trees that each should be concatenated, from
     * left to right. It turns a chained call like "a".+("b").+("c") into
     * a list of arguments.
     */
    def (GenICode.this.global.Tree)List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]liftStringConcat(GenICode.this.global.Treetree: GenICode.this.global.TreeTree): List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]List[Tree] = GenICode.this.global.Treetree List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]match {
      List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]case Apply(GenICode.this.global.Selectfun @ Select(GenICode.this.global.Treelarg, GenICode.this.global.Namemethod), List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]rarg) =>
        List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]if ((GenICode.this.global.Symbol)BooleanisPrimitive(GenICode.this.global.Selectfun.=> GenICode.this.global.Symbolsymbol) (Boolean)Boolean&& 
            object GenICode.this.global.scalaPrimitivesscalaPrimitives.(GenICode.this.global.scalaPrimitives.global.Symbol)IntgetPrimitive(GenICode.this.global.Selectfun.=> GenICode.this.global.Symbolsymbol) (Int)Boolean== scalaPrimitives.Int(100)CONCAT)
          (GenICode.this.global.Tree)List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]liftStringConcat(GenICode.this.global.Treelarg) (List[GenICode.this.global.Tree])List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]::: List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]rarg
        else
          (GenICode.this.global.Tree*)List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]List(GenICode.this.global.Treetree)
      List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]case _ =>
        (GenICode.this.global.Tree*)List[GenICode.this.global.Tree]List(GenICode.this.global.Treetree)
    }


    /**
     * Traverse the tree and store label stubs in the context. This is
     * necessary to handle forward jumps, because at a label application
     * with arguments, the symbols of the corresponding LabelDef parameters
     * are not yet known.
     *
     * Since it is expensive to traverse each method twice, this method is called
     * only when forward jumps really happen, and then it re-traverses the whole
     * method, scanning for LabelDefs.
     *
     * TODO: restrict the scanning to smaller subtrees than the whole method.
     *  It is sufficient to scan the trees of the innermost enclosing block.
     */
    private def (GenICode.this.global.Tree,ICodePhase.this.Context)UnitscanForLabels(GenICode.this.global.Treetree: GenICode.this.global.TreeTree, ICodePhase.this.Contextctx: ICodePhase.this.ContextContext): UnitUnit =
      template $anon extends GenICode.this.global.Traversernew GenICode.this.global.TraverserTraverser() {
        override def (GenICode.this.global.Tree)Unittraverse(GenICode.this.global.Treetree: GenICode.this.global.TreeTree): UnitUnit = GenICode.this.global.Treetree Unitmatch {

    /**
     * Generate the "==" code for object references. It is equivalent of
     * if (l eq null) r eq null else l.equals(r);
     *

     * @param r       right-hand side of the '=='

    /** Does this tree have a try-catch block? */
    def (GenICode.this.global.Tree)BooleanmayCleanStack(GenICode.this.global.Treetree: GenICode.this.global.TreeTree): BooleanBoolean = {
      var BooleanhasTry = Boolean(false)false
      template $anon extends GenICode.this.global.Traversernew GenICode.this.global.TraverserTraverser() {
        override def (GenICode.this.global.Tree)Unittraverse(GenICode.this.global.Treet: GenICode.this.global.TreeTree) = GenICode.this.global.Treet Unitmatch {
          Unitcase Try(_, _, _) => BooleanhasTry = Boolean(true)true
          Unitcase _ => super.(GenICode.this.global.Tree)Unittraverse(GenICode.this.global.Treet)
        }
      }.(GenICode.this.global.Tree)Unittraverse(GenICode.this.global.Treetree);
      BooleanhasTry
    }

    /** Tree transformer that duplicates code and at the same time creates
     *  fresh symbols for existing labels. Since labels may be used before
     *  they are defined (forward jumps), all labels found are mapped to fresh
     *  symbols. References to the same label (use or definition) will remain
     *  consistent after this transformation (both the use and the definition of
     *  some label l will be mapped to the same label l').
     *
     *  Note: If the tree fragment passed to the duplicator contains unbound
     *  label names, the bind to the outer labeldef will be lost! That's because
     *  a use of an unbound label l will be transformed to l', and the corresponding
     *  label def, being outside the scope of this transformation, will not be updated.
     *
     *  All LabelDefs are entered into the context label map, since it makes no sense
     *  to delay it any more: they will be used at some point.
     */
    class class DuplicateLabels extends GenICode.this.global.Transformer with ScalaObjectDuplicateLabels(scala.collection.Set[GenICode.this.global.Symbol]boundLabels: collection.scala.collection.Set[GenICode.this.global.Symbol]Set[Symbol]) extends GenICode.this.global.TransformerTransformer {
      val scala.collection.mutable.Map[GenICode.this.global.Symbol,GenICode.this.global.Symbol]labels: scala.collection.mutable.Map[GenICode.this.global.Symbol,GenICode.this.global.Symbol]Map[Symbol, Symbol] = scala.collection.mutable.HashMap[GenICode.this.global.Symbol,GenICode.this.global.Symbol]new scala.collection.mutable.HashMap[GenICode.this.global.Symbol,GenICode.this.global.Symbol]HashMap
      var GenICode.this.global.Symbolmethod: GenICode.this.global.SymbolSymbol = _
      var ICodePhase.this.Contextctx: ICodePhase.this.ContextContext = _

       * with a context where all the handlers are active. Handlers are 
       * evaluated in the 'outer' context. 
       *
       * It returns the resulting context, with the same active handlers as
       * before the call. Use it like:

       * <code> ctx.Try( ctx => { 
       *   ctx.bb.emit(...) // protected block

       *   ctx => { 
       *     ctx.bb.emit(...); // exception handler
       *   }), (AnotherExceptionClass,
       *   ctx => {...
       *   } ))</code>

    /** 
     * Represent a label in the current method code. In order
     * to support forward jumps, labels can be created without
     * having a deisgnated target block. They can later be attached 
     * by calling `anchor'.
     */
    class class Label extends java.lang.Object with ScalaObjectLabel(val GenICode.this.global.Symbolsymbol: GenICode.this.global.SymbolSymbol) {
      var Booleananchored = Boolean(false)false
      var GenICode.this.global.icodes.BasicBlockblock: GenICode.this.global.icodes.BasicBlockBasicBlock = _
      var List[GenICode.this.global.Symbol]params: List[GenICode.this.global.Symbol]List[Symbol] = _

      private var List[GenICode.this.global.icodes.Instruction]toPatch: List[GenICode.this.global.icodes.Instruction]List[Instruction] = object NilNil

      /** Fix this label to the given basic block. */
      def (GenICode.this.global.icodes.BasicBlock)GenICode.this.Labelanchor(GenICode.this.global.icodes.BasicBlockb: GenICode.this.global.icodes.BasicBlockBasicBlock): GenICode.this.LabelLabel = {
        (Boolean,=> Any)Unitassert(=> Boolean!=> Booleananchored, java.lang.String("Cannot anchor an already anchored label!")"Cannot anchor an already anchored label!")
        (Boolean)Unitanchored = Boolean(true)true
        Label.this.typethis.(GenICode.this.global.icodes.BasicBlock)Unitblock = GenICode.this.global.icodes.BasicBlockb
        GenICode.this.Labelthis

    /**
     * Pseudo jump: it takes a Label instead of a basick block.
     * It is used temporarily during code generation. It is replaced
     * by a real JUMP instruction when all labels are resolved.
     */

      override def => Intconsumed = Int(0)0
      override def => Intproduced = Int(0)0

      // register with the given label

        GenICode.this.Labellabel.(GenICode.this.global.icodes.Instruction)UnitaddCallingInstruction(GenICode.this.PseudoJUMPthis);
    }
